GT: c0*epsilon**c1 + c2*(T - c3)*exp(-epsilon)

I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the ground truth:

**GT: 7.317*epsilon^3 + 7.950*(T - 287.09)*exp(-epsilon)**

This simplifies to: `c0*epsilon^3 + c2*T*exp(-epsilon) - c2*c3*exp(-epsilon)`

So the GT has three basis functions: **epsilon^3**, **T*exp(-epsilon)**, and **exp(-epsilon)**.

Let me analyze each candidate systematically.

### Candidate 1:
`c0*exp(T*c1) + c2*exp(T*c3) + c4*exp(c5*|epsilon|) + c6 + c7*exp(T*c3)*exp(c5*|epsilon|)`

Basis functions: exp(T*c1), exp(T*c3), exp(c5*|epsilon|), constant, exp(T*c3 + c5*|epsilon|). 
GT needs epsilon^3 and T*exp(-epsilon). There's no polynomial term in epsilon and no linear T dependence. Setting c1=0 gives a constant, not T. Cannot match.
**Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 2:
`c0*epsilon^c1 + c2*epsilon^c3 + c4 + c5*exp(c6*sin(T*c7 + c8*epsilon + c9))`

The last term involves exp(sin(...)), which cannot produce T*exp(-epsilon). No match.
**Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 3:
Everything is divided by (c1 + epsilon) and involves T linearly and exp(T*c7). GT has T*exp(-epsilon), not T times rational functions of epsilon. The exp(T*c7) terms can't produce exp(-epsilon). No match.
**Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

Similar structure to Candidate 3. Same reasoning.
**Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

Has exp(c3/(T+c4)) which gives exp(1/T)-type dependence, not linear T. Cannot produce T*exp(-epsilon).
**Candidate 6 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

**Candidate 7 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 15:
`c0*epsilon^3 + c1*exp(T*c2 + c3*epsilon) + c4*epsilon^c5 + c6 + c7*exp(T*c8)`

Basis functions: epsilon^3, exp(T*c2 + c3*epsilon), epsilon^c5, constant, exp(T*c8).

GT = c0*epsilon^3 + c2*T*exp(-epsilon) - c2*c3*exp(-epsilon)

The term exp(T*c2 + c3*epsilon) = exp(T*c2)*exp(c3*epsilon). This is NOT T*exp(-epsilon). It's exponential in T, not linear in T. No match.
**Candidate 15 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 21:
`c0*epsilon^c1 + c2*exp(T*c3)*exp(c4*|epsilon|) + c5*epsilon^c6 + c7 + c8*exp(T*c3)`

With epsilon ≥ 0, |epsilon| = epsilon. So:
= c0*epsilon^c1 + c2*exp(T*c3)*exp(c4*epsilon) + c5*epsilon^c6 + c7 + c8*exp(T*c3)
= c0*epsilon^c1 + (c2*exp(c4*epsilon) + c8)*exp(T*c3) + c5*epsilon^c6 + c7

GT needs T*exp(-epsilon), which is linear in T. exp(T*c3) is exponential in T. Cannot match.
**Candidate 21 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 22:

exp(T*c2) is exponential in T, not linear. No match.

### Candidate 53:
`T*c0*exp(T*c1) + c2*epsilon/(c3+epsilon) + c4*exp(T*c5) + c6*epsilon*exp(T*c1)`

This gives T*c0 (linear in T but no epsilon dependence in the T term). GT needs T*exp(-epsilon). No match.

---

After careful analysis, the GT requires **linear dependence on T** (specifically T*exp(-epsilon)), but virtually all candidates have either no T dependence, exponential T dependence (exp(T*c)), or other non-linear T dependence (log(T+c), exp(c/T), T/(T+c), etc.). None can exactly reproduce T*exp(-epsilon).
